<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделить.html>отдели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otdelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделять.html>отделя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otdeljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделить.html>отдели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to separate, to detach, to part</li>
<li>to disjoint, to divorce, to separate off</li>
<li>to divide, to serve as boundary</li>
<li>to secrete</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ля.html>ля́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> vent, something that gives relieve to frustrations</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ду́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ши<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-отдуш-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ин</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***отдых.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдых.html>о́тдых</a> (2236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдых.html>о́тдых</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótdyx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдых.html>о́тдыха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдых.html>о́тдыхи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдых.html>о́тдыхов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rest</li>
<li>relaxation, respite</li>
<li>holiday (in the sense of vacation)</li></ol>

***отек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отек.html>отёк</a> (7538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отек.html>отёк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otjók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отек.html>отёка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отек.html>отёки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отек.html>отёков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>edema, dropsy, hydrops, hypostasis</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***отец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a> (177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*otьcь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*átta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otéc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>father
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">крёстный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krjóstnyj <b>otéc</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">godfather</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:духовный.html>духо́вный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">duxóvnyj <b>otéc</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">confessor <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see also духовник, исповедник</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svjatój <b>otéc</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">priest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">посажённый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posažónnyj <b>otéc</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(at a wedding) proxy, sponsor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>мать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otcóv mnógo, a matʹ odná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there are many fathers but only one mother</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвалиться.html>хвали́сь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцо́м</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвалиться.html>хвали́сь</a> сы́ном-молодцо́м</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne xvalísʹ <b>otcóm</b>, a xvalísʹ sýnom-molodcóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don’t be proud of father, but take pride in a good son</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">муж <a href = vnd.unilang:жена.html>жене́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:жена.html>жена́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муж.html>му́жу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:венец.html>вене́ц</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">muž žené <b>otéc</b>, žená múžu venéc</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a husband is a father to his wife, and the wife is a crown for him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ancestor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцы́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знавать.html>знава́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приказать.html>приказа́ли</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otcý</b> náši étovo ne znaváli i nam ne prikazáli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">our ancestors didn’t know of this and didn’t guide us.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> senior, superior, first of, chief, sensei
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">арара́т-гора́ — <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>гора́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ararát-gorá — vsem gorám <b>otéc</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mount Ararat is the father of mountains</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>familiar term of address for an elderly man</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> referring to a man who cares about sоmеbody or something like a father
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родной.html>родно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak rodnój <b>otéc</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">like one’s own father</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ад.html>ада́м</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>ро́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человеческий.html>челове́ческого</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Adám — <b>otéc</b> róda čelovéčeskovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Adam is the Father of man</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ста́лин — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Stálin — <b>otéc</b> naródov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stalin is the father of the nations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> founder, initiator of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">да́рвин — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теория.html>тео́рии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:эволюция.html>эволю́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dárvin — <b>otéc</b> teórii evoljúcii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Darwin is the founder of the theory of evolution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:врачебный.html>враче́бной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otéc</b> vračébnoj naúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">father of medicine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">about Hippocratus</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">отцы́-основа́тели</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otcý-osnováteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Founding Fathers</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> root, basis, source
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">санскри́тский <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языко́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:европейский.html>европе́йских</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sanskrítskij jazýk — <b>otéc</b> jazykóv jevropéjskix</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Sanskrit is a root of the Indo-European languages</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:догадка.html>дога́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nuždá <b>otéc</b> dogádki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">necessity is the mother of invention</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">need is the father of wit</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́чество</a> (5869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́чество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otéčestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́чества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́чества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́честв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fatherland, motherland, native land, native country, country</li>
<li>mother country, home country, homeland</li></ol>

***отжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отжать.html>отжа́ть</a> (24347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отжать.html>отжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отжимать.html>отжима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to squeeze dry</li>
<li>to squeeze out (liquid)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push back, to drive back, to force to retreat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force to separate under pressure (e.g. a valve, a layer of rock)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extort, to expropriate, to seize or take the possession of something by physical force, menace or other illegal and ingenuine means</li></ol>

<ol><li>to finish harvesting, to finish reaping</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отжимать.html>отжима́ть</a> (25146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отжимать.html>отжима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otžimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отжать.html>отжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to squeeze dry</li>
<li>to squeeze out (liquid)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push back, to drive back, to force to retreat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force to separate under pressure (e.g. a valve, a layer of rock)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extort, to expropriate, to seize or take the possession of something by physical force, menace or other illegal and ingenuine means</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отзыв.html>отзыв</a> (9333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отзыв.html>о́тзыв</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótzyv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отзыв.html>о́тзыва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отзыв.html>о́тзывы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отзыв.html>о́тзывов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>opinion, review, response, comment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отзыв.html>о́тзыв</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ótzyv</b> o čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a review of something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>reference, testimonial</li>
<li>response, echo</li>
<li><i>(to the password)</i> reply</li></ol>

***отзывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отзывать.html>отзыва́ть</a> (27706)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отзывать.html>отзыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otzyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отозвать.html>отозва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to recall, to summon <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">political or diplomatic personnel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отзывать.html>отзыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посла́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otzyvátʹ</b> poslá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to recall/summon</b> the ambassador</span></div></dd>

<li>to speak <i>(of)</i>

<li>to tell <i>(upon, on)</i></li>
<li><i>(pain)</i> to extend <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отзывать.html>отзыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otzyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
